AOSP Changelogs

KVT49I to KTU78B speculative commit log.

This is a unconfirmed commit log based off a file which appeared in the AOSP and was subsequently removed.

The commits IDs are from a repository which is not currently publicly accessible and so direct-to-commit links aren't available.
